# Push sustainable backspin-vs-backspin rally calibration (return-studio.html)

> Research tool output (return-studio.html), not game4.html acceptance. Does not modify return-studio.html.
Updated: 2026-07-13T12:50:49.936Z
Presets: 11 (11-preset calibration set, same exclusions as push-tilty-sweep-calibration.js: no_spin_long_forehand, no_spin_long_backhand, backspin_short_forehand_2, backspin_short_backhand_2, backspin_short_backhand)
maxRounds per rally: 12. Backspin threshold on canonical outgoing topspin: <= -15.

## Design principle under test

Push should PRESERVE/REGENERATE backspin, not neutralize it — a legal push-vs-push rally should be able to continue indefinitely with the ball staying in backspin. Prior finding (push_rally_round2_failure_diagnosis.txt): deployed config neutralizes canonical incoming topspin (~-70..-83) to near-zero (~-3..-4) at contact, flipping to genuine topspin (~+31..+33) by round 2, killing rallies at round 2.

## Grid dimensions (two-stage, per split of driveScale into independent liftScale/driveScale)

liftScale multiplies PUSH_LIFT_BASE's output only (vertical racket velocity); driveScale multiplies PUSH_DRIVE_BASE's output only (forward racket velocity). Their ratio is the racket's own swing-direction angle (deployed baseline: atan(0.35/0.7)=26.57° from horizontal); their magnitude is overall swing speed. tiltY (paddle face angle) is independent of both.

- Stage 1: tiltY x liftScale x driveScale = 3 x 4 x 4 = 48 combos x 11 presets x up to 12 rounds each. TANGENT_KP/PADDLE_FRICTION held at deployed values (1/0.4).
  tiltY candidates: 0.8, 1, 1.2
  liftScale candidates: 0.5, 0.8, 1.1, 1.4
  driveScale candidates: 0.3, 0.5, 0.7, 0.9
- Stage 2: TANGENT_KP-scale x PADDLE_FRICTION = 4 x 4 = 16 combos, tiltY/liftScale/driveScale fixed at stage-1 winner (tiltY=1.2 liftScale=1.4 driveScale=0.5 angle=54.5° TANGENT_KP=1 PADDLE_FRICTION=0.4).
  TANGENT_KP-scale candidates (x deployed 1): 1, 1.5, 2, 3
  PADDLE_FRICTION candidates: 0.4, 0.6, 0.8, 1

## Backspin threshold empirical check

Threshold: canonical outgoing topspin <= -15 classified as "backspin"/isBackspin=true. Agreement rate between isBackspin(round i) and round i's contact being legal (net+inbounds), aggregated over baseline+stage1+stage2 (65 combos x 11 presets x up to 12 rounds):

- survived & backspin: 143
- survived & NOT backspin: 1420
- failed & backspin: 42
- failed & NOT backspin: 618
- agreement rate: 0.3423 (isBackspin==true predicting survival, isBackspin==false predicting failure)
